             <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 12.0pt; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: 6.0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-align: justify; line-height: 150%;">
              <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
               <span style="font-size: 14.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif';">
                <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                 1.
                 <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </strong>
              <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
               <span style="font-size: 14.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif';">
                Establishment
               </span>
              </strong>
              <br/>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; color: black; mso-themecolor: text1;">
               The college has established with three departments in 2011/12 namely Computer Science, Information Technology and Information System and the fourth one Software Engineering in 2013/14 and all of them are currently enrolled students and provide teaching learning activities. Currently, the college is carrying out its undertakings with a total of 107 staffs. By now the college has a total of 1121 regular undergraduate students.
              </span>
              <br/>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; color: black; mso-themecolor: text1;">
               The vision of the College is to serve students and the community through excellent learning programs, by conducting relevant and effective research and community engagement projects.
               <br/>
               The College commits itself to the achievement of academic excellence in the field of computing and informatics. To this end, it offers various program ranging from undergraduate to doctoral level.
               <br/>
               Our graduates will be in demand from industry and from higher education institutions all over Ethiopia and the world. It will be well recognized all over the world due to its many publications and due to the works of its centers of excellence.
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; color: black; mso-themecolor: text1;">
               In line with its expansion procedures the college will strive to succeed the delivery of quality education, problem solving research undertakings and its community services.
               <br/>
               Whatever your stage of education, we have the expertise to take you to the top. We are well established in the higher education market and have gained the reputation as a leader in computing.
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-left: .25in; mso-add-space: auto; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1;">
              <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
               <span style="font-size: 14.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif';">
                <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                 2.
                 <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </strong>
              <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
               <span style="font-size: 14.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif';">
                Objectives
               </span>
              </strong>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo2;">
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               Produce qualified and competent man power in the field of computing and informatics.
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo2;">
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               Enable students under take demand oriented and problem solving research and development activities.
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo2;">
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               Develop managerial and entrepreneurship skill of students to start their own computing business.
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo2;">
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               Equip students to organize and provide in-service and society training program related with computing
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo2;">
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               To equip students with necessary knowledge and skill of writing, reporting and communicating for scientific paper
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo2;">
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               Inspire students to have a positive attitude towards their profession to have the sense of cooperation, honesty and loyalty
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo2;">
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               Provide consultancy and advisory service, skill up-grading trainings and community development services.
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo2;">
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               Produce socially accountable personnel who would give alternative solutions to socioeconomic problems.
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo2;">
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               To promote the concept of comprehensive and multidisciplinary approach in tackling computer related problems.
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo2;">

                <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                 <span style="font-size: 11.5pt; font-family: 'Arial','sans-serif'; mso-fareast-font-family: Arial; color: #0d0d0d; mso-themecolor: text1; mso-themetint: 242; letter-spacing: .4pt;">

                   </span>

                 </span>

              <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 12.0pt; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: 6.0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-align: justify; line-height: 150%;">
               <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; color: black; mso-themecolor: text1;">
                Admission requirements would be similar to the general institutional requirements. That is, the student should complete preparatory level education and the entry point is determined accordingly by the Ministry of Education for the regular students whereas the admission criteria for distance and continuing education program are as per the Universitys requirement.
               </span>

               </a>
               <span style="mso-bookmark: _Toc364342883;">

                 <span style="font-size: 11.5pt; font-family: 'Arial','sans-serif'; mso-fareast-font-family: Arial; color: #0d0d0d; mso-themecolor: text1; mso-themetint: 242; letter-spacing: .4pt;">
                  <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                   .
                   <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </strong>
                <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                 <span style="font-size: 11.5pt; font-family: 'Arial','sans-serif'; color: #0d0d0d; mso-themecolor: text1; mso-themetint: 242; letter-spacing: .4pt;">
                  Duration of the Study
                 </span>
                </strong>
               </span>
              </p>
              <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 12.0pt; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: 6.0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-align: justify; line-height: 150%;">
               <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; color: black; mso-themecolor: text1;">
                Students will not take different computing courses at their high school study. The nature of the disciplines needs many practical works considering the above facts, objectives, under normal circumstances,
                <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                 <em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">
                  <span style="text-decoration: underline;">
                   four years
                  </span>
                 </em>
                </strong>
                of study are required to complete the all programs.
               </span>
              </p>
             </div>

               <span style="font-size: 14.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif';">
                <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                 6.
                 <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </strong>
              <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
               <span style="font-size: 14.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif';">
                Strategic Directions
               </span>
              </strong>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; text-align: justify; mso-pagination: none;">
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               The college has four departments that those focus on the following:
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo4;">
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                1.
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               ICT services include laboratory service
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo4;">
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                2.
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               Software Development and Innovations
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo4;">
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                3.
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               Finance and External Linkage
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo4;">
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                4.
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               Research and Community Service
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo4;">
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                5.
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               Human Resource Development both in number and upgrading
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo4;">
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                6.
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               Academic Programs and Quality Assurance.
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="margin-left: .25in; mso-add-space: auto; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l5 level1 lfo1;">
              <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
               <span style="font-size: 14.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif';">
                <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                 7.
                 <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </strong>
              <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
               <span style="font-size: 14.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif';">
                Special Features of Learning at CCI
               </span>
              </strong>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-top: 7.0pt; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-left: .5in; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo5;">
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               Promoting an interactive atmosphere with follows students and lecturers.
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-top: 7.0pt; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-left: .5in; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo5;">
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               Excellent level of academic support.
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-top: 7.0pt; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-left: .5in; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo5;">
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               Continuous assessment system used throughout all programs in order to better prepare for end of semester final examinations by learning in a progressive manner.
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-top: 7.0pt; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-left: .5in; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo5;">
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               Career-based programs aligned closely with developments and changes in the IT global industry.
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-top: 7.0pt; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-left: .5in; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo5;">
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               After-car academic tutorial support provided by lecturers outside regular class time.
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-top: 7.0pt; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-left: .5in; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo5;">
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               Class demonstrators used in practical lectures to help more students understand lab demonstrations.
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-left: .25in; mso-add-space: auto; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l5 level1 lfo1;">
              <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
               <span style="font-size: 14.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif';">
                <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                 8.
                 <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </strong>
              <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
               <span style="font-size: 14.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif';">
                Colleges Facilities
               </span>
              </strong>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-top: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-left: .75in; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l6 level1 lfo6;">
              <span style="font-size: 14.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               Fully wireless and wired Internet access.
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-top: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-left: .75in; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l6 level1 lfo6;">
              <span style="font-size: 14.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               Fully equipped computer laboratories.
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-top: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-left: .75in; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l6 level1 lfo6;">
              <span style="font-size: 14.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">
                
                <span style="font: 7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               Access to a PC and Laptop computers for all academic staffs.
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="margin-top: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-left: .75in; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l6 level1 lfo6;">
              <span style="font-size: 14.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-ligatures: none;">
               <span style="mso-list: Ignore;">

               </span>
              </span>
              <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 130%; font-family: 'Times New Roman','serif'; mso-ligatures: none;">
               Access teaching materials on local ftp server.
              </span>
             </p>
             <p>
             </p>
             <p>
             </p>
             <p>

             <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; mso-add-space: auto; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-pagination: none; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo2;">

    $jsmart(document).ready(function($){  
		/* Begin: add class pattern for element */
		var headerbgimage = 'pattern_8';
		var footerbgimage = 'pattern_5';
		if(headerbgimage){
			$('#yt_header').addClass(headerbgimage);
			$('#yt_slideshow').addClass(headerbgimage);
		}
		if(footerbgimage){
			$('#yt_footer').addClass(footerbgimage);

	});

   <a href="#" id="yt-totop">
    Scroll to top
   </a>
   <script type="text/javascript">
    $jsmart(function($){
		// back to top
		$("#yt-totop").hide();
		$(function () {
			var wh = $(window).height();
			var whtml =  $(document).height();
			$(window).scroll(function () {
				if ($(this).scrollTop() > whtml/10) {
					$('#yt-totop').fadeIn();
				} else {
					$('#yt-totop').fadeOut();
				}
			});
			$('#yt-totop').click(function () {
				$('body,html').animate({
					scrollTop: 0
				}, 800);
				return false;
			});
		});
		// end back to top
	});
   </script>
